Paper Currency Redemption Process

Gong Yu Has Redeemed Eight-Tenths

County Government Auctions the Property of Four Money Shops

Xuzhou Correspondence: The Xubu paper currency surge that stirred up a wave before the New Year, during County Magistrate She's tenure, had required the Gong Yu Bank, jointly formed by merchants, to fully redeem. At that time, Gong Yu shareholders raised funds to issue small denomination notes for redemption, but ultimately, it was difficult to raise cash, and redemption was soon suspended. Since Wang Gongyu took over as County Magistrate, he has been striving for a thorough clean-up, taking responsibility on his behalf, and borrowing 30,000 yuan for Gong Yu from the banking community, 20,000 yuan for Bu Xinji, and 10,000 yuan for Yi Zhenxiang. As a result, these three families opened for redemption before the New Year. However, Chunquan, Tian Baoyu, Shixingchang, and Juhechang, four families, were unable to mortgage due to a lack of credit guarantees. They are currently engaged in auctioning off the property of these four families for an initial redemption at a discount. To date, seven banks have been able to enter the path of a complete resolution, and private banknotes can be expected to disappear from this point on. The handling of the redemption process is recorded below.

The Redemption Process of Three Banks: Gong Yu Bank was jointly formed by large and small shops in this port, Bu Xinji was a large grocery store on Daoping Road in the South Gate, and Yi Zhenxiang was a wine and oil workshop on Zhongzheng Street in the East Station. Gong Yu had large merchants among its shareholders responsible, while Bu Xinji and Yi Zhenxiang, in addition to all their industries, also had their relatives and friends privately participating in the responsibility. This is why they were able to gain the trust of the bank, and with the County Government using administrative power to sign a guarantee contract, they respectively borrowed cash and opened for unlimited redemption before and after the end of the lunar year. The slight easing of the market at the end of the lunar year was entirely dependent on this. Gong Yu was 30,000 yuan, Bu Xinji 20,000 yuan, and Yi Zhenxiang 10,000 yuan. To date, about eight-tenths have been redeemed. When redemption first opened, large amounts were redeemed every day. After the New Year, they were as rare as morning stars. Currently, merchants and residents in the city have no notes from these three families. Even farmers in the countryside, or those further away from Xuzhou, are unlikely to hold many notes. Based on this speculation, this 60,000 yuan in cash is sufficient to cover the total amount needed to clear the three families. Gong Yu reported that the amount of notes was 140,000 yuan. When shareholders raised funds to issue small denomination notes for redemption, some had already been recovered. During the initial run, daily limited redemption also recovered some. Bu Xinji and Yi Zhenxiang issued fewer notes to begin with, and the limited redemption during the initial economic redemption also recovered a lot. In the past two months, those who had creditor relationships with the note issuers have also purchased paper notes at a discount to repay debts. In addition, the paper notes outside were inevitably lost and damaged, so a small amount of funds can achieve the effect of clearing. Currently, the three families are still continuing to redeem, and no problems are expected to occur in the future.

Auctioning the Property of Four Banks: Chunquan, Tian Baoyu, Juhechang, and Shixingchang, four families, were rejected by the bank due to a lack of credit guarantees, and the County Government could not take responsibility on their behalf. The County Government had ordered the owners of the four families to quickly find their own solutions, but the County Government remained in a position of assistance. However, since the four families have not been able to devise a plan to date, the County Government believes that further delays are unacceptable and plans to auction off their property. However, in terms of valuation, the difference is too great. It is also planned that after the auction, the cash obtained will be redeemed at a discount according to the proportion of the total amount. However, this type of debt is different from ordinary debt and cannot be settled at a bankruptcy discount. Therefore, it is planned that when redeeming at a discount, a seal will be added to the original note, which will still be kept by the note holder, and when the note owner has continued financial resources, a full redemption will be made, not only so that the public will not suffer losses, but also to prevent the occurrence of private banknotes in the future. The County Government has issued a notice to clear the property of the four families, which states: "It has been found that the notes of Tian Baoyu, Chunquan, Shixingchang, Juhechang, and other four families have been unresolved for a long time, which has greatly affected the interests of the public. This government has repeatedly ordered the note holders of the four families to quickly raise funds for redemption, but they have not complied. In order to seek a quick solution, the property of the four families will be actively cleared and prepared for sale for redemption. Anyone who has information about the property of the four families, in addition to those that have been sealed and registered by this government, or those who have hidden or failed to report, are now allowed to report within two weeks so that this problem can be resolved as soon as possible. Let all sectors of the public know." As for the property of the four families that has been sealed and registered, Chunquan has 12 qing of farmland in Yuzhuang in the seventh district, and 8 qing of land on Gushan in Xiaojing. Tian Baoyu has 217 mu of farmland in Wangdian in the fifth district, 35 mu of farmland at Broken Bridge in the fifth district, 100 mu of land west of Shijiazhuang in the first district, a house on the old Daoshu Street, a house south of the electric light factory, and two mu of the Hongmiao city base. Shixingchang has 300 mu of farmland in Xiaohuangjia in the fifth district, 335 mu of official farmland, two houses in Zhou Dongxiang, a market house on Sidao Street, (Guang Chunquan pawned) half of a pit house, (Wanhua Yong pawned) a house on Fushu Street, (Hongxing Yong pawned) Suhechang has 50 mu of farmland in Yanjiashan in the seventh and eighth districts, 50 mu of Daliao land, 150 mu of Wangjiashan land, and a house in Mahao Town. (14th)

Anhui Province

Building a Hall and Lending Funds to Repair Dikes

Allocating 200,000 of Sheyu Road Public Bonds

Raising Cash to Lend to Various Counties for Application

Anqing Correspondence: The main dikes of the Yangtze and Huai Rivers in Anhui Province were previously commissioned by the Construction Department to send a large number of supervisors to various sections to recruit workers for construction. However, the construction costs were enormous, and the National Economic Council delegated the task to Anhui Province to raise funds on its own. However, Anhui Province's treasury was in dire straits, and it was not easy to raise funds quickly. Now, in order to assist in the construction of the main dikes of the Yangtze and Huai Rivers, and to repair the breaches of the inner dikes connecting the main dikes, the Construction Department has allocated 200,000 yuan of Sheyu Road public bonds, raised cash, and lent it to various counties for application. After careful investigation of the actual situation of various counties along the Yangtze and Huai Rivers, and the local economic conditions and tax revenue ratios, Huaining and 19 other counties were ordered to subscribe for sales separately, with the largest amount being 20,000 yuan and the smallest only 2,000 yuan. The provincial government has been presented with orders for the counties to pay the amount in installments, and a method for lending funds for dike repair has been drafted, designating the dike repair counties as Huaining, Tongcheng, Wuwei, Hexian, Dangtu, Wuhu, Fanchang, Tongling, Guichi, Dongliu Susong, Wangjiang, Fuyang, Yingshang, Huoqiu, Fengtai, Huaiyuan, Lingbi, Fengyang, and Wuhe, a total of 20 counties. The amount of the loan is allocated by the Construction Department according to the needs of the projects in each place, and distributed by the county magistrates of each county in conjunction with the supervisory committee to distribute the loans to each embankment or small section, and an examination committee is organized to submit it for examination and approval. The loan is charged at 8% interest per annum. Starting from the Republic of China year 24, the principal and interest will be repaid once every three and nine months, with the interest decreasing along with the principal. The principal and interest will be publicly shared by each county in the benefited fields according to the amount borrowed by each embankment section, divided into six installments, and paid to the county for collection on schedule until the loan is repaid in full. The Loan for Dike Repair Examination Committee is composed of seven members, with one person each from the Provincial Government Secretariat, the three departments of civil affairs, finance, and construction, and the Water Conservancy Engineering Office, and two members of the Provincial Disaster Relief Committee are invited to form the committee. The committee is attached to the Construction Department for convenience and cost savings. (March 14)

Songjiang

County Government Re-Divides Districts in Detail

The Department of Civil Affairs previously ordered the various counties to re-divide the districts in order to reorganize the autonomous regions. Yesterday, the county government convened a meeting of district chiefs, bureau chiefs, etc., chaired by County Magistrate Jin, who reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, opinions on district division were put forward. After public deliberation, it was decided that the 16 districts in the county would be merged into 8 districts. According to the district map and population division, the new first district will be the area of the old first district, second district, tenth district's Litawei Beiqian Loujiabang, and three townships, and the third district's Chedun Yinjiabang Jinzengbang Yanlian Xinzhen Zhongjing Qianputang Jiangjia Shiqiao Zhang Liqiao Liuleimiao, and ten townships. The district office will be located in the county seat. The new second district will be the area of the old third district, seventh district, and the sixth district's Zhaozhuang Gushulong Xingye Jia Bang, and four townships. The district office will be located in Sijing. The new third district will be the area of the old fourth district, fifth district, and the sixth district's Zhang Zhuang North Xia Bang Sun Jia Bang, and three townships north of the railway. The district office will be located in Wujiatang in the old fifth district. The new fourth district will be the area of the old eighth district, ninth district, and the tenth district's Zhang Zhuang North Xia Tang Sun Jia Bang, and three townships north of the railway. The district office will be located in Xiao Kunshan. The new fifth district will be the area of the old eleventh district and the tenth district's Hengliaojing, and each township map south. The district office will be located in Fengjing. The new sixth district will be the area of the old thirteenth district and fourteenth district. The Taying Township of the old thirteenth district will be merged into this district. The district office will be located in Yexie. The new seventh district will be the area of the old twelfth district of Tinglin. The district office will be located in Tinglin. The new eighth district will be the area of the old fifteenth and sixteenth districts. The Nantang Town of the twelfth district will be merged, and the Shu Hu Township of the old sixteenth district will be merged into the new seventh district. After the division of each district, the county will instruct the district offices of each new district and the reorganized townships of the original districts to convene district affairs meetings to discuss and submit them for approval.

Kunshan

Bandits Rob and Kidnap

Qian Zhaokun, a villager in Zhujing outside the East Gate, is said to be well-off, which has been coveted by bandits. In October of last year, Qian received a letter from bandits demanding a large sum of money. Qian ignored it. At 3:00 AM on the 14th, more than ten bandits suddenly broke down the door, speaking with mixed accents and holding wooden sticks. They immediately searched for silver dollars, but were not satisfied. They then kidnapped Qian's daughter-in-law, Ms. Fang. At this time, County Magistrate Peng Baichuan learned of this and immediately ordered Inspector Wang Shuren of the Public Security Bureau to lead police captain Luo Qixiang and police to rush to pursue the bandits. The bandits had already fled far away. They immediately returned to Kunshan to report. The escaped bandits are now being strictly pursued, and the hostage is being rescued.

Taicang

Execution of Robber by Firing Squad

On the night of November 24th last year, at about 8:00 PM, Wang Weishen's home, a farmer in Huchuan Township, District 1, was robbed, and the victims, Wang Weishen and others, were burned with candles. Later, the Kunshan County Defense Corps intercepted Zhang Ronggui and seven others. The county government of this county welcomed them back to Taicang and interrogated them repeatedly. Zhang Ronggui confessed to jointly robbing and injuring people and obtaining stolen goods. According to the victim's clear identification in court, he was sentenced to death according to law and reported to the provincial government. On the morning of the 14th, the prisoner Zhang Ronggui was signed and escorted, his identity was verified, and he was tied to the execution ground for execution by firing squad.

Qingpu

Robbery and Injury in Qijian Village

Zhang Shuhua, of Qijian Village in District 7 of the county, is a small business owner, and the bandits are coveting him. He was previously kidnapped and lost thousands of dollars before he escaped danger. He then moved to the city to avoid danger, and several years have passed. Last year, in order to save expenses, he moved back home. Unexpectedly, dozens of bandits suddenly came to his home and broke down the door on the evening of the other day. They forbade him from making any noise and searched arbitrarily. At that time, Shuhua was unable to escape and was beaten by the bandits with fists and feet, causing serious injuries. It is estimated that clothing and other items worth hundreds of dollars were robbed. The three neighboring families of Zhang Zeshu, Zhang Hanming, and Zhang Xingsheng also suffered similar robberies.

Suzhou

County Education Directors Gather in Suzhou for Discussion

The education directors of various counties in Jiangsu Province, in view of the fact that the Department of Education intends to propose 20% of the education funds and various special education funds of each county as the general reserve fund of each county, if implemented, will have a great impact on the future of education in each county. Therefore, it was decided to gather at the Wuxian Education Bureau on the 24th of this month to discuss all matters.

Wuxi

Major Water Robbery: Police and Bandits in Fierce Battle

Recently, the atmosphere in the four townships has been uneasy, and news of robbery has been frequent. On the afternoon of the previous day (14th) at about 5:00 PM, five ships from this county to Qingyang Nan Zha Jin Tong Bridge and Changzhou Henglin jointly departed from Wuxi. At about 7:00 PM, as dusk fell, they approached Gaokou. Suddenly, more than ten burly men on the shore, holding guns and flashlights and speaking with mixed northern accents, opened fire and ordered the ships to stop. The five ships, seeing the situation was not good, immediately stopped. At that time, Patrol Leader Liu Yulin, who was stationed on the ship, led the police to protect the ship. Upon hearing the alarm, he remained calm and silently directed the police to crawl ashore in the dim light. At his command, they raised their guns and returned fire. The bandits also opened fire. The two sides fought fiercely for about ten minutes. At the same time, the Qianqiao Defense Corps also heard the alarm and arrived to assist in the battle. In the end, the bandits were overwhelmed and retreated backwards. Patrol Leader Liu immediately ordered the entire team of police officers to surround and pursue the bandits. The bandits fled in all directions. Two bandits jumped into the river and were chased into the water by the police and captured. Another bandit was also captured. The guns carried by the bandits were thrown into the river. The remaining bandits all escaped. Patrol Leader Liu then ordered the police to tie up the three captured bandits and escort them to the Water Patrol Detachment, and then transfer them to the county government for legal action. It is said that one bandit was killed in the police-bandit battle and his body fell into the river, but this has not been confirmed. In addition, on the afternoon of yesterday at about 6:00 PM, a Su Xi ship, which had departed from Wuxi and was heading to the Xiadian Bridge near Mianzhangjiang Bridge, was suddenly met by a fishing boat, and three bandits jumped out, each holding a handgun, a pudao, and other weapons, and boarded the ship to search. At that time, there were two water police officers from the first squad of the ninth team of the second district of the water police on board, carrying weapons to protect the ship. Upon hearing the alarm, they attempted to resist, but because there were more bandits, they were instead robbed of a gun and 38 rounds of ammunition. The silver dollars and goods on board were also looted, resulting in significant losses. In addition, a Xi Chang ship was also robbed under the Suokou Bridge at about 8:00 PM the previous night, with losses of over 100 yuan. Now, the shipping industry, seeing the danger on the water, has jointly petitioned the county government to request protection for navigation and to strictly pursue the stolen goods.

Yinjiang

Current Status of the Zhencheng Road Project

Since the provincial government ordered the Zhencheng Road to be paved, all counties along the line have started construction. Cheng County has completed eight or nine tenths of the project. The National Economic Council specially appointed Xu Xingfang to conduct an inspection along the road with Wu Tingzuo, the director of the engineering office. Only one-half of the first section of Zhenjiang has been completed, and the remaining sections have only been completed by three or four tenths. The Danyang section has only been slightly paved last year, and has not yet started construction this year. The Wujin section also has poor results. The Jiangyin section is the best, and the entire road has been completed by eight or nine tenths. After completing the inspection, the Xu Committee and others went to Shanghai.

Jiading

Change of Prison Staff

Huang Ruyuan, the county government's prison warden and director of the detention center, has previously served in the Jiangsu Fourth and Second Sub-Prisons and has rich experience. After taking office last month, he found that the number of prisoners in the county's prison was large, overcrowded, and had deep-seated problems that were difficult to reform. He immediately requested resignation from the High Court and was approved by order. Liu Fu was appointed as the successor, and Liu took over on the 10th.

Changzhou

County Government Executes Bandit Leader in Kidnapping Case

On January 6th of this year, at 8:00 PM, Wu Jinquan's home, a resident of Shijiatang, Yongning Township, District 16 of Wu County, was suddenly entered by bandits who searched the room and kidnapped Wu's son, Yuan Sheng, and hid him in the home of a bandit in Liuyi Township, demanding a large sum of money for ransom. Later, Wu Yuansheng took the opportunity to escape home. The police regiment of the district, along with informants, went to the bandit's lair to search and arrested many bandits, including Zong Koulin, who was confirmed to be the ringleader in the case. The county government sentenced him to death and reported to the provincial government for approval. On the afternoon of the 14th, the police were dispatched to sign and escort the prisoner to the case, verify his identity, tie him to the Fengweidun execution ground, and execute him by firing squad.

Jiaxing

Adding a Bus Station at Wangwu Bridge

The bus station on the Jiaxing-Suzhou-Jiaxing Highway is located at Chemen, but the prosperous commercial market of Jiaxing is in Beimen. Passengers who come to Jiaxing by bus have to get off at the station and then go to Beimen, which is time-consuming and uneconomical. Therefore, merchants and residents in the Shuangqiao area have jointly petitioned the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction to set up a bus branch station at Wangwu Bridge in Beimen to facilitate travel. The Jiangsu Construction Department ordered the Suzhou-Jiaxing Highway Administration to investigate. It has now been decided to approve the addition of a branch station. The station address is in the Yilifeng Hotel west of Wangwu Bridge, and Mr. Xu has been appointed as the manager. Ticket sales will begin on March 16th.

Local News

Jardine Matheson's Yisheng Ship Robbed by Pirates

Robbery Along the Fujian-Guangdong Coast Lasts More Than 30 Hours

Ten Passengers Kidnapped, Losses of Passengers and Goods Unknown

The Company Received a Telegram Yesterday Stating That the Ship Had Arrived in Hong Kong

Jardine Matheson's Nanhua liner Yisheng, which was chartered from a Norwegian company in Hong Kong, was originally named Norviken. After being chartered by Jardine Matheson, it was renamed Yisheng and operated on the Nanhua route, also calling at Qingdao. On the 11th of this month, it left Shanghai fully loaded with yarn, cloth, flour, rice, groceries, etc., totaling more than 20,000 pieces, as well as 11,000 pieces of soybean cake bound for Shantou, and a number of passengers, departing Shanghai at noon.

Pirates Disembark in Shanghai

Before the ship weighed anchor in Shanghai, a group of pirates, disguised as passengers, boarded the vessel. Yesterday, the company received a telegram stating that there were twenty-two pirates in total. On Tuesday (the 13th) at approximately 6 a.m., as the ship approached the waters off Fuzhou, the pirates emerged, each wielding firearms. Several pirates stormed the bridge and the radio room, driving the crew into one room under guard. After cutting the radio antenna and throwing it into the sea, they began their looting spree, sparing neither crew nor passengers. They also opened the cargo holds and seized goods. Two other pirates, on the bridge, forced the captain to steer the ship towards the

northern part of Dapeng Bay, to a place called (Chlang) (transliteration). By 3 p.m. on Wednesday, the 14th, they reached their destination. The pirates had pre-arranged everything, so as soon as the ship arrived, a pirate ship approached and the stolen goods were unloaded onto it.

Ten Passengers Kidnapped

In total, the pirates' plundering lasted from 6 a.m. on the 13th to 3 p.m. on the 14th, spanning over thirty hours. As they were about to leave, dissatisfied with their loot, they kidnapped ten passengers. The names of those kidnapped and the value of the stolen goods are currently under investigation, hence the telegram did not provide further details.

Request for Search and Suppression After the Incident

After the pirates left, the captain bypassed Shantou and sailed directly to Hong Kong. He arrived in Hong Kong yesterday and reported the hijacking to the head office. The head office immediately telegraphed Shanghai and also telegraphed British warships along the coast and our national authorities, requesting them to dispatch ships to search and suppress the pirates and rescue the kidnapped passengers.

Flying Club

Preparatory Office to be Established

Formal Establishment Pending Central Approval

Representatives from Military, Political, and Other Sectors Scheduled to

Confer This Afternoon on Venue Arrangements for the Tianchu Aircraft Naming Ceremony

Regarding the establishment of the Flying Club and the Tianchu aircraft naming ceremony, Mr. Lin Wo-jiang, Secretary-General of the Chinese Aviation Association, stated yesterday that the organizational outline of the Flying Club had been drafted. However, as this type of organization is a new endeavor in our country, all plans require careful consideration. A special telegram has been sent to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for instructions. Once central approval is obtained, the formal establishment can proceed. To facilitate progress, it is planned to establish a preparatory office around the 18th of this month. The Tianchu aircraft naming ceremony is scheduled to take place on the 18th at the Hongqiao Airfield. The government has dispatched Xu Pei-gen, Director of the Aviation Administration, as its representative to Shanghai to accept the aircraft. The Executive Yuan will send Mr. Chu Minyi as its representative to attend. The order of the ceremony will be: first, the Tianchu aircraft naming ceremony; second, the presentation of the Sun Tonggang aircraft by Du Yuesheng; and third, the acceptance of the secondary title for the Tianchu aircraft and the presentation of the aircraft by Sun Tonggang by the Aviation Association. Regarding venue arrangements, security, and traffic control, the Aviation Association's office will convene a meeting this afternoon at 4 p.m. at the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, inviting representatives from the Municipal Government, Public Security Bureau, Public Works Bureau, Security Department, and Tianchu Factory to discuss all matters. A dispatch from Nanjing states that Sun Tonggang will travel to Shanghai on the evening of the 15th to accept the "Pengcheng Wanli" aircraft donated by Du Yuesheng. He is scheduled to depart from Shanghai by that aircraft on the morning of the 19th to fly to Beijing. After a one-day stopover, he will fly back to his hometown in Shandong on the original aircraft. At the end of the month, he will fly from Shandong to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for instructions, and he plans to go abroad in early June.

American Aviator

Hawke to Depart for Guangzhou This Morning

Giant Bomber Being Transported to Hangzhou by Waterway

After One Month of Assembly and Testing, Will Return to Shanghai for Performance

American aviator Mr. Hawke, after bringing the Condor giant bomber to Shanghai, once went to Hangzhou for inspection and returned to Shanghai the night before last. He will take the China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) flight to Guangzhou this morning around 7 a.m. As for the Condor aircraft, due to the difficulty in railway transportation, it will be transported to Hangzhou by waterway on Sunday. The assembly and testing will take a considerable amount of time. According to a representative of Curtiss-Wright Corporation to the New Voice News Agency, it will take thirty days to complete and then return to Shanghai for performance. Details are as follows:

Flying to Guangzhou This Morning　After arriving in Shanghai, Hawke went to Hangzhou with Mr. Paul, the Shanghai representative of Curtiss-Wright Aircraft Company, for inspection some days ago. He returned to Shanghai from Hangzhou the night before last. According to Paul to the New Voice News Agency yesterday, the two of them will take the CNAC Shanghai-Guangzhou southbound flight to Guangzhou from Longhua at 7 a.m. this morning and will return to Shanghai in about a week. Pilot Coles will not be traveling with them.

Land Transportation Obstacles　The Condor aircraft is very large. Paul and Hawke originally intended to transport the aircraft to Hangzhou for assembly and testing, because the Hangzhou airfield has a larger space for placing the aircraft. However, the bridges and steel frames on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway are narrower, and the aircraft could not pass on a train. As a result, problems arose. They then wanted to transport the aircraft to the Hongqiao Airfield for installation, but the bridges near Nanyang University on the way can only accommodate objects weighing five tons, while the minimum weight of the Condor aircraft is eleven tons. Therefore, that was also impossible. It was also suggested to transport the aircraft to the Longhua Airfield, and there were no problems with transportation, but the hangar at that airfield, after the Condor aircraft was installed, could not be moved out due to the increased size of the fuselage. Therefore, neither location was suitable for assembly and testing.

Water Transport to Hangzhou　It is now known that the aircraft has been handed over to a transportation company for shipment. According to Paul to the New Voice News Agency, it has now been decided to transport the aircraft to Hangzhou by waterway on Sunday (the day after tomorrow) for assembly and testing, which will take a total of thirty days to complete and then return to Shanghai for performance.

Bankers Acknowledge

Increasing Taxes is the Only Solution to Silver Prices

Adopting the Gold Standard is Ideal but Difficult to Achieve

China Cannot Prohibit Silver Exports Due to its Trade Deficit

New Voice News Agency reports that the United States' implementation of raising silver prices has gradually affected the commerce of silver-using countries around the world. China, as one of the silver-using countries, is no exception. As for the countermeasures to be taken, it was rumored among foreigners in Shanghai yesterday that China was advocating taking this opportunity to adopt the gold standard. However, according to the New Voice News Agency's inquiries from various parties, the government has no such intention. It may be the opinion of private parties. It would certainly be a good strategy to cope with rising silver prices, but it is difficult to achieve in reality. Banks in Shanghai generally believe that the only solution is to increase the silver export tax and that prohibition of exports is not possible. It is said that the total amount of silver in China is only 150 million, and foreign merchants hold two-thirds of the total, which is alarming. Details are as follows:

Difficult to Change Standard

Yesterday, news circulated among foreign banks in Shanghai that, in order to deal with the United States' increase in silver prices, China is now considering taking this opportunity to implement the gold standard in accordance with Kemal's gold standard plan report, so that Chinese native products will not be affected by the increase in silver prices. From the perspective of gold-using countries, increasing silver prices means increasing commodity prices. If China switches to the gold standard, then the prices of Chinese goods will also increase with the silver price. However, according to the New Voice News Agency's inquiries from domestic banks, the government currently has no such intention, believing that this proposal may be the opinion of private parties and stating that this proposal cannot be said to be bad, but it is difficult to implement in practice. China lacks the raw materials to switch to the gold standard, which is the biggest difficulty, and it is more costly, which cannot be done in China's current period of economic crisis. Therefore, Dr. Kemal's report cost the Ministry of Finance more than one million in expenses and can only be regarded as reference material to this day.

Only Taxation Can Cope

Since it is difficult to switch to the gold standard, the only way to cope with rising silver prices is to increase the corresponding silver export tax to restrict it. Leading figures in the Shanghai banking industry, such as Bei Songsun, Xu Jiqing, Zhang Gongquan, Li Fusun, Xu Xinliu, and Lin Kanghou, all agree with this proposal. However, the increase in the silver export tax must be based on the extent to which the United States raises silver prices. For example, if the current difference between the silver price raised by the United States and the Chinese silver price is 5 percent, then China's export tax should also be increased by 5 percent from the original 2.5 percent export tax to balance it. However, if silver prices fall, the export tax must also be reduced to restrict it.

Cannot Prohibit Silver Exports

The banking community also believes that it is impossible to prohibit silver exports. Prohibiting silver exports would cause panic in society, so this matter is absolutely impossible. China has a large trade deficit, averaging 700 million per year. If silver exports are prohibited, then this 700 million trade deficit, which is the foreign goods purchased by Chinese merchants, will not be paid. Moreover, the exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar will become more expensive, and the price of silver in China will fall, which will cause great panic. Private smugglers of silver will also have huge profits to be made. At that time, it may be impossible to prohibit smuggling, and the outflow of silver may still occur naturally. Therefore, the banking community also believes that this proposal is impossible.

Alarming Silver Deposits Held by Foreign Merchants

According to people in the banking industry yesterday, the total amount of silver in Shanghai, including Chinese and foreign banks and money shops, is 150 million taels, and the silver held by foreign banks, such as HSBC and Standard Chartered Bank, accounts for two-thirds of the total, which is 100 million taels. The remaining 50 million is owned by Chinese merchants, of which the money shops account for only 5 million. Chinese merchants can be assured, but silver held by foreign banks may inevitably flow out. When reporters inquired about this news yesterday, they heard that the total amount of silver in Shanghai was 150 million taels. Subsequently, according to other leading figures in the banking industry, the 150 million silver deposits are actually the total amount of silver collected in Shanghai by banks across the country.

Minting is Also a Good Strategy

In addition, the banking community believes that using silver to mint silver coins to counteract the outflow of silver is also a good strategy. If the minted silver coins are melted down again for silver and transported for export, it would be too uneconomical. Therefore, after silver is minted into silver coins, it should not flow out. However, the mint currently only mints more than 200,000 coins per day, which is a drop in the bucket and is of little help.

Foreign Pilotage Rights

No Treaty Stipulations

Chinese Pilots Association Issues Statement

Central News Agency reports that recently, there have been rumors that the Shanghai Consular Corps, due to the Chinese government's proposal to recover the entire pilotage sovereignty, considered the issue to be significant and convened a meeting to discuss it. The consular corps believes that pilotage sovereignty is part of inland navigation rights and that it is difficult to resolve the pilotage rights issue before the inland navigation rights issue is resolved. It is said that the consuls have already requested instructions from their home countries. Now, according to a statement issued by the Chinese Pilots Association, the pilotage sovereignty of our country is completely different from inland navigation rights and is two separate matters. The only basis for foreigners to be pilots is the pilotage regulations approved by the General Customs Commissioner Robert Hart to the Prime Minister's Office during the seventh year of Tongzhi of the Qing Dynasty. The largest and most important Shanghai South Entrance Pilotage Company, which is now occupied by foreigners, is also organized based on the above regulations. Not only does the association have the company's articles of association, but the government also has records. It is now a forced and groundless association. Since foreigners have been pilots in our country, they have aided the enemy and funded the enemy, such as in the battles of Tanggu, Mawei, and January 28, and the damage has been unbearable. Therefore, we are determined to recover it in order to protect ourselves. Moreover, what was approved in the seventh year of Tongzhi was not a treaty, but a government order on internal affairs. Now, changing the previous order with a later order will not be subject to any foreign interference. Therefore, our reasons are very sufficient, and the other party has no way to deal with it, so it involves unrelated matters in an attempt to expand the dispute in order to restrain it. The ignorant are spreading this news in order to shift the psychology of the people of the country, which is regrettable. According to the association's observation, all meetings are just superficial. The National Government issued the pilotage regulations in September last year. If each country had reasons to object, why did the problem not arise until today? It is hoped that the people of the country will pay attention to this in the future, such as the claim made by foreigners

Liu Xiang Denies Slander by Japanese Newspaper

Telegram to Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek and Chen Cheng

The National News Agency reports that the Japanese newspaper "Shanghai Nichinichi Shimbun" has slanderous reports on Sichuan affairs. Liu Xiang, Commissioner of Bandit Suppression in Sichuan, telegraphed Wang Jingwei and Chiang Kai-shek on the 13th of this month. The original telegram is disclosed on the right (brief): "Secret, recent telegram to Chiang Kai-shek and Wang Jingwei: 'According to a telegram from the staff stationed in Shanghai yesterday, the Shanghai Nichinichi Shimbun's report on Sichuan affairs is extremely slanderous, especially against Xiang. It says that he harbors ambitions, eliminates dissidents, or has other conspiracies that are detrimental to the central government. It even says that Xiang is colluding with Britain and France to build a railway to connect to Pianma. All kinds of rumors are unfounded. Xiang is ordered to suppress bandits and plan for rehabilitation. He is grateful for the support of your honor, wants to save the people of Sichuan from misery, his ability is small and his responsibility is heavy, and he is always afraid of failing. Seeing the devastation and displacement of the local people, he feels restless. He can only work hard to suppress and stabilize the country in order to repay your kindness. He knows nothing else. As for the schemes of manipulation and exclusion, Xiang despises and hates them the most. The national power is declining to the extreme. Joint efforts to save the country are still feared to be insufficient. The hardships are beyond the understanding of outside newspapers. As for the development and construction, Xiang is determined to do so. He has hired specialists to investigate local resources as preparation for future development and the elimination of bandits and the reduction of troops. This is the responsibility of rehabilitation. There is no conspiracy and no need to collude with foreigners. The Shanghai Nichinichi Shimbun is run by the Japanese, and its wanton slander has other intentions. The foreign newspapers and a certain news agency in Shanghai have echoed and spread the rumors. I am afraid that many people will believe the lies and not be able to distinguish between truth and falsehood. Xiang briefly describes the situation and hopes for your understanding. Sincerely, Liu Xiang.' The former."

Saying that pilotage is related to treaties is just a smokescreen. (The following omitted)

Yellow River Relief Committee Disaster Relief Group

Scheduled to End This Month

All Funds Transferred to Public Works Relief

Central News Agency reports that regarding the Disaster Relief Group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, yesterday morning, a reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Xi De-jiong, director of the group, at the committee. According to him, Mr. Kong Xiangxi, chairman of the committee, has ordered the group by telegram to temporarily end at the end of March due to financial difficulties, so that all funds can be used for public works relief. The current state of disaster relief is recorded as follows.

Relief Agencies Temporarily Closed

According to Xi, after the establishment of the Disaster Relief Group, investigation and distribution bureaus were established in the disaster areas of Shandong, Hebei, and Henan provinces, and personnel were dispatched to various disaster areas to provide relief. Many refugees were rescued, and the amount of money used to date has reached more than one million yuan. Mr. Kong Xiangxi, chairman of the committee, decided to temporarily suspend the work of the Disaster Relief Group at the end of March because public works relief in the three provinces had not yet been completed, and it would be more effective to send personnel to provide relief after the completion of the works, and because the committee's finances were in difficulty, so that all the committee's funds could be used for public works relief. After the breaches of the Yellow River in the three provinces have been completely blocked and completed, the situation will be reviewed in order to provide relief. After receiving the order, the group notified the relief agencies set up in the three provinces, such as refugee reception centers, porridge factories, and investigation and distribution bureaus, to close down in stages within the time limit.

Refugees on the North Bank of the Yellow River Awaiting Rescue

Xi continued that although the disaster situation in the three provinces has gradually improved compared to the past, there are still many refugees awaiting rescue. The disaster area on the south bank of the Yellow River was less affected, and the breach was blocked long ago, so there is no problem. However, the refugees on the north bank are still in dire straits. Those in urgent need of relief are the nine counties of Puyang and Dongchang in Shandong, Changyuan in Hebei, and Hua County and Yanjin in Henan. The situation is still extremely tragic, because the area of the breach on the north bank is large. Therefore, the solution to the disaster should be to block the breach first so that the Yellow River can return to its old course. It is heard that the Public Works Relief Group has already started blocking the breach and aims to complete it in the short term.

Transferring Refugees to the Northwest for Reclamation

Since the disaster in the three provinces, the local elites have been almost completely lost. The Yellow River Disaster Committee has decided to send the refugees awaiting rescue in the area to various places. After this plan to transfer refugees is decided, it will be coordinated with the provinces to which they are sent. An agreement has been reached with the Ministry of Railways regarding the free transfer of refugees. It is very good to transfer the homeless refugees to the northwest for reclamation and it is hoped that it can be done. It is also known that Xi plans to visit Kong in Beijing after Kong returns to Beijing from Jiangxi to present everything in person because the Disaster Relief Group is about to end.

Shanghai Merchants and Factories Enthusiastically Participate

Achievements of Shanghai Factory National Goods in Hankou

Rushing to Transport Two Batches of Goods to Hankou

The Shanghai Citizens' Promotion of National Products Association, at the invitation of Mayor Wu of Hankou, led the Shanghai National Products Traveling Delegation, and united with more than 120 well-known national products manufacturers in Shanghai, to participate in the Hankou Municipal National Products Mobile Exhibition. It is heard that all representatives of the delegation and factory staff arrived in Hankou at 7 a.m. on the 9th, and were welcomed by representatives from all walks of life in Hankou to Xinhua Company for a rest. They immediately responded to the public banquets of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and various groups, and were very busy with the banquets in recent days. The venue was arranged by the political and business associations, and the order was well-organized. The Shanghai factories occupied 108 rooms on the first and second floors, and the Hankou factories occupied 50 rooms on the third floor. The exquisite national goods were gathered together, with colorful and dazzling brilliance. At noon on the 10th, Mayor Wu hosted a banquet for the manufacturers and held a welcome meeting. There was a lot of toasting and the guests and hosts enjoyed themselves. During the meeting, the mayor gave a grand speech, saying that promoting national products can not only block the leaks, but also enrich the country and strengthen the people. It is the only great plan to save the country at present, and asked everyone to work hard to do it. At 2 p.m. on the 11th, the opening ceremony was held. In the melodious sound of military music, Mayor Wu's wife unveiled the curtain. Local military and political leaders were present to deliver speeches. The situation was extremely enthusiastic, and the visitors were even more crowded, causing many glass windows to be crushed. The daily business in the Shanghai factory was calculated to be more than 20,000 yuan, which was an unprecedented grand occasion for the delegation. Therefore, the representatives of the Shanghai factory had a letter and telegram to transport two more batches of goods to Hankou, which shows that the people in the area are enthusiastic about using national goods and that the cooperation between the political and business sectors is appropriate, so there are such achievements. Yesterday, the standing committee members of the Citizens' Promotion of National Products Association, Yu Qiaqing, Xu Jianruo, Chen Binghui, Wu Zhihao, Hu Xiyuan, and Fang Jiange, held a standing committee meeting and resolved to notify all factories to rush to transport two batches of goods to meet the needs of Hankou.

Shanghai Municipal Council

Discussing the Problem of Rickshaws

On the afternoon of the 14th of this month, the Public Works Bureau's Security Committee and Vehicle Affairs Committee held a joint meeting to discuss the issue of rickshaws. All attendees were members and staff of the Public Works Bureau. Yesterday's (15th) newspaper reported that the rickshaw trade association had nominated Yin Zhiling and Gu Songmao to attend the Public Works Bureau to request participation, but after repeated consideration by the Public Works Bureau, they were immediately allowed to do so, which is inaccurate.

The *North-China Daily News* reported that the joint meeting of the Security Committee and the Transportation Committee convened last night. It is said that a resolution was reached to request the Public Works Bureau to take direct action to implement most of the articles listed in the Marseille Report. During the discussion of the articles, all those who expressed their views were eager for the Public Works Bureau to take action as soon as possible. As for the proposal put forward by the Marseille Committee to organize a rickshaw company to operate independently, without contact with existing rickshaw companies, it was also thoroughly studied at the time. However, whether this proposal can prove to be the most practical solution, there is still no certainty.

The *Shanghai Evening Post and Mercury* reported that the Public Works Bureau Council will convene on Wednesday next week. It is said that the council members generally agree to limit the daily rental fee for rickshaws to eight jiao (cents) in small foreign currency. If there is excessive profit-taking, the rickshaw license will be revoked as a warning. This is almost certain, according to the Sichuan merchant community.

Opposing the Price Increase of Shanghai-Chongqing Steamers

Stopping business as a form of resistance

The Chongqing Hardware and Sundries Trade Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday stating that the current alliance price increase of Shanghai-Chongqing steamers is as high as two or three times, and the lowest is also 100%. Moreover, the old habit of deducting hair has been completely destroyed, resulting in freight exceeding the cost of goods, which is too numerous to mention. This kind of arbitrary and crude action is unanimous. They felt that the Sichuan commercial situation has been extremely depressed. What could further devastate the already withered flower? Moreover, with the national humiliation yet to be avenged, all sectors of the country should work together to resist foreign aggression. Now, the Shanghai-Chongqing steamers ignore public interests and harm others for their own benefit. If Japanese ships intend to resume navigation, this opportunity will be seized to facilitate the profiteering of fishermen. This is like providing the enemy with weapons and provisions and is insane. Therefore, yesterday, a joint meeting of various Shanghai merchant guilds was held, and everyone was indignant. The atmosphere in the entire venue suddenly became tense. As a result, a unanimous decision was made to suspend business from today onwards as a form of resistance. They vowed not to sell Shanghai goods to Chongqing again until the original price target was restored. The members of our association unanimously believe that the commercial situation has been extremely depressed in recent years, and the pain has been particularly severe. They strongly support this resolution. The business of our association is closely related to the agricultural and industrial sectors. Now that production and construction are established as national policies, if, in addition to the depressed situation, there is also exploitation by water transport costs, then the direct destruction of our fellow traders will be a minor harm. The indirect impact on the agricultural and industrial sectors will hinder the major plan of establishing the country, and the future of the Republic of China will be unthinkable. Therefore, this special letter is sent, and it is requested that your association be enthusiastic and assist in arguing according to reason, aiming to restore the original price. It is heard that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has already forwarded the letter to the Shipping Trade Association for verification.

The company handled the customs declaration and the Wusong Office of the Shipping Office, requesting inspection and registration on file. Unexpectedly, at about 2:00 PM, an inspector from the Shipping Office suddenly came to Wusong and went to the Wanxing ship to investigate, falsely claiming that the Wanxing ship had concealed tonnage dues and imposed a fine of 40 yuan. The ship owner, feeling unjustly penalized, could not submit and came to the company to request that someone be sent to explain. The company immediately sent Lin Jinsheng to explain with the ship owner. Unexpectedly, the ship inspector Wang Chunsen and others were unreasonable and not only did not accept the company's explanation but also violently beat the company's employee Lin Jinsheng. Not satisfied with the beating, they also arbitrarily detained him in the ship, sent him to Shanghai, forced him to sign a document, and detained him for six hours before releasing him. Checking the national taxes and fees is the duty of the people. Now that the ship owner has already reported and requested registration, there is nothing illegal or unreasonable. Forcibly imposing an additional penalty is naturally unacceptable. The company sent someone to request a re-examination, which is also a legitimate procedure. Now, being unjustly assaulted and detained is not only an injustice suffered by the company, but also the future ship merchants will be in an unthinkable situation. Therefore, it is specially reported to the Shanghai Municipal Government to send someone to investigate, to extend grievances, etc. According to this, the Jinwanxing ship is loading and transporting fish to Wusong. All the reporting, fee registration procedures have been completed. Even if the Shipping Office inspector discovers concealed or missed fee matters, he should also declare the facts, which is enough to show obedience. Now, wide abuse of the penalty, sent by the customs reporting company, the staff went to state, but also unreasonable, without unauthorized assault, followed by detention, the employee's this act, in fact, ultra vires, severe suffering merchants, should be investigated according to the law, Lihe according to the situation presented, begging Junfu Jianhe, prompt Ciling went to check the truth, by cleaning up the official administration and Anliang cowardly, in fact, for the public cloud.

Sinking of Cargo Ship by Yongji Warship Case

Navy Headquarters Refuses Compensation

Only Willing to Give Shipowner Xu Laofu 100 Yuan

On January 19th of this year, Xu Laofu's iron barge was sunk in the Huangpu River by the Yongji warship, and the ship and cargo were lost. Xu Laofu's family of six, old and young, were fortunately seen and rescued by Dr. Hua Du's ship. Afterwards, the Copper and Iron Trade Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, requesting a special letter to the Navy Headquarters, demanding compensation for the losses, to relieve the difficulties of the merchants, etc. This was reported in the newspapers. This case has not yet been resolved. Shipowner Xu Laofu made a living by loading barges with goods. The whole family lived on the ship. All the savings and furniture for making a living were lost in the water. Once the ship was sunk, food, clothing, housing, and transportation were lost. Although the empty barge has been salvaged, there is no strength to carry out repairs. If the purpose of compensation is not achieved, the whole family will not be able to survive. The situation is very tragic. He has repeatedly complained to the association, and the association has suffered the sinking of 16 tons of pig iron, except for the two tons and three kilograms that have been salvaged. The estimated loss is about 900 yuan. All of them are required to be compensated. On the 20th of last month, Municipal Chamber of Commerce member Zhu Wenqi, together with Copper and Iron Trade Association members Zhang Zilian, Feng Xinmin, and Wu Jiaze, took shipowner Xu Laofu to the Gaochang Temple Navy Headquarters to discuss a solution. Captain Ouyang received them and shipowner Xu Laofu presented the situation of the collision and requested compensation for the losses. Captain Ouyang blamed the shipowner for being careless, resulting in the collision and sinking, and it was difficult to compensate. Considering the plight of the shipowner, he only agreed to give 100 yuan. Municipal Chamber of Commerce member Zhu Wenqi and Copper and Iron Trade Association members Zhang Zilian and others believed that the amount was too different and could not comply. The captain immediately resolutely stated that he could only ask the court to resolve the matter, and the gentlemen immediately said goodbye. It is regrettable that the captain only spoke officialdom and did not speak facts. The Copper and Iron Trade Association has continued to send letters to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, asking for justice to be upheld and the purpose of compensation achieved, to maintain the difficulties of the merchants.

The Meiya Factory Labor Dispute Remains Unresolved

Authorities Decide on Handling Measures

According to the Dagong News Agency, more than 4,000 workers from the Meiya Silk Weaving General Factory and its various branches went on strike to protest against wage reductions. The following is the latest news as of yesterday:

Laborers Petition

Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the workers of the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory sent more than ten representatives, including Cai Shoufu from the general factory, Kong Qingxian from the second factory, Feng Xianchun from the third factory, Lü Haiquan from the fourth factory, Xia Zhiwei from the fifth factory, Zhu Linchai from the sixth factory, Yu Yilai and Cai Hangsong from the seventh factory, He Yayun from the eighth factory, Sun Zhifen and Tong Chunqi from the ninth factory, Liu Yanqing from the tenth factory, and Pan Yuncai, to the Fenglinqiao Municipal Party Department to petition, requesting assistance so that the matter could be resolved as soon as possible. They were received by Long Peiyun, a staff member of the Civil Movement Section, and Yu Yaoqiu, a staff member of the Investigation Section, who inquired about the cause of the strike and the details of the wage cuts. They promised to investigate the matter together with the Bureau of Social Affairs and then find a way to mediate, hoping that the workers would wait patiently for a resolution and not take any actions that would go beyond the bounds. The workers expressed satisfaction and left.

Company Notice

The Meiya Silk Factory issued a notice setting a deadline for workers to resume work, stating that the workers' strike had been repeatedly advised to resume work as soon as possible, but to no avail. It has now exceeded ten days, which not only violates factory rules but also violates government laws and regulations. It is now limited to the 17th of this month to resume work as usual. Do not wait and delay, otherwise it will be regarded as an automatic dismissal in accordance with Articles 26, 3 and 4 of the factory rules approved by the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. It should be dismissed uniformly and new workers should be recruited. Do not mistake yourself. This announcement,

Party and Government Measures

The Municipal Party Department and the Bureau of Social Affairs, considering the serious situation of the Meiya Silk Factory labor dispute, were deeply afraid of causing further incidents. Therefore, at 2:00 PM yesterday, the Municipal Party Department sent Long Peiyun, a staff member of the Civil Movement Section, and Yu Yaoqiu, a staff member of the Investigation Section, to the Meiya General Distribution Office on Tianjin Road to investigate the details, together with Zhu Guilin, a staff member of the Third Section of the Bureau of Social Affairs. They also issued a joint order to the workers to resume work first, and ordered the factory to postpone the wage reduction and mediate quietly.

The Kungwo Steamer Changes to Using "Compradors"

Tea Boys Hold a General Meeting Yesterday

Decided to Ask the Seafarers' Union to Negotiate According to Law

The British-owned Jardine Matheson Steamship Company plans to change the official cabins of the Kungwo steamer into second-class large dining rooms and reduce the number of workers (tea boys) in the middle cabins and hire stewards (i.e., "compradors") in order to develop its business, which has caused disputes. All the tea boys held a meeting yesterday to discuss how to deal with the situation. Details are recorded below:

Negotiation Failed

The British-owned Jardine Matheson Steamship Company has dozens of ships. The company, considering that the business of the official cabins of each ship is not as developed as that of the large dining rooms, has changed the official cabins of the Jiwo, Lungwo, and Suiwo steamers into second-class large dining rooms. Recently, it also wanted to reform the Kungwo steamer and planned to dismiss all the tea boys and hire "compradors," which caused opposition from the workers. The Seafarers' Union repeatedly negotiated, but the company said that the tea boys were not familiar with English and could not be appointed, so there was no result.

Tea Boys' Meeting

The ship employs about 90 tea boys. Hearing this news, they believed that the company's move was tantamount to destroying the entire tea boy livelihood. The masses were indignant and convened a general meeting of all tea boys at the Grand Auditorium of the Seafarers' Union in Wengjia Branch Lane, Ximen, at 1:00 PM yesterday. Representatives from the union and various ships attended. The meeting was chaired by Yu Dequan. The results of the discussion were: (1) Ask the General Branch of the Seafarers' Union to negotiate according to law; (2) Unite to resist. The representatives of the ships believed that the matter was closely related, so they all expressed their willingness to be a backup.

Cotton Control Commission Plans to Establish

Henan Cotton Production Improvement Branch

Xu Zhongdi and Others Have Been Appointed to Proceed

3,000 Odd Loads of High-Quality Seeds Have Already Been Delivered

Henan Province has a wide cotton-producing area. Except for the Lingbao area in western Henan and the Zhangde area in northern Henan, which have better quality, the rest, such as the Taikang area in eastern Henan, mostly have poor seeds, low yields, and extremely uneven quality, so the selling price is very low. When the cotton is harvested, farmers are eager to sell it, and middlemen monopolize it, so cotton farmers work hard all year round but earn little. The Cotton Control Commission of the National Economic Commission, in view of this, specially sent technical experts Xu Zhongdi and Feng Zefang to Henan to prepare for the establishment of the Henan Cotton Production Improvement Branch, first engaging in improvement and promotion and organizing cooperatives in the Taikang, Qixian, and Suixian areas. The association also appointed Lu Chengzhou as the acting director of the Henan Cotton Production Improvement Branch, Xu Xingmin as the cotton planting instructor of the branch, and Wang Yijiao as the soil cultivation instructor of the branch. In addition, there are several assistants. The Cotton Control Commission received a report from Special Commissioner Xu yesterday, stating that he had visited Director Zhang of the Construction Department on the morning of the 13th, and the result was very satisfactory. In the afternoon, the Construction Department transferred two vehicles from the Highway Bureau for Special Commissioner Xu and others to use for surveying the site in the Qixian, Suixian, and Taikang areas. As for the high-quality seeds, more than 3,000 loads have arrived from Zhangde, enough to plant more than 50,000 mu of cotton fields. In the future, they will gradually be promoted to benefit the farmers of Henan Province.

Inside the Datong Hotel

Robbers Apprehended After Dividing Loot

Victim Appears in Court to Testify

Robbers Admit to Committing Robbery

The robbers, Chen Qiaosheng from this locality, Chen Zhongyi from Ningbo, Li Agui, Zhao Zuji, and Chen Linsheng, along with accomplices carrying weapons, went to the home of Xu Qilin, a Shaoxing native, at No. 21, Lane 796, Beijing Road around 8 a.m. the day before yesterday. They robbed him of jewelry and silver worth 540 yuan. They hid in rooms 235 of the Great Eastern Hotel on Yinhua Street, Nanjing Road, and were about to divide the loot when Wei Quanfu, the Chinese Chief Detective of the Hongkou Police Station, discovered their whereabouts. Together with Detective Zhu Jihuang, Detective Wang Zhusheng, Wang Debiao, and Detectives Zhang Desheng and Zhang Yaoji, and Western detectives, they secretly went to the hotel. At the address, they arrested Chen Qiaosheng and the other four men. Under the sofa cushions, they found three handguns and 24 bullets. In the bedding, they found three original watches, two rings, 31 silver dollars, 24 silver dollars, 82 double-coin pieces, and two single-coin pieces. Four gold forks, one gold bracelet, and eleven silver chopsticks were taken away by accomplices. All were taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The lawyer from the Public Works Department, Wang Yaotang, stated that the case was initiated by the defendant Chen Zhongyi. Chen Linsheng found out that the victim's family had valuables. They met and discussed the plan at the Sutai Hotel and the Yile Tian Tea House. Chen Linsheng went to Xu's residence to identify it. Chen Zhongyi waited at the Great Eastern Hotel, while the other defendants carried out the robbery. The defendants confessed at the police station. He requested a postponement for further investigation. Most of the original stolen jewelry and silver were presented for inspection. According to the victim Xu Qilin, his daughter-in-law Zhu, and the rickshaw driver Yuan A'er, they testified about the robbery. Judge Wu Zehan questioned each of the defendants and ordered them to be remanded in custody for further investigation at a later date.

Xu Leqing Kidnapping Case

Wu Ziqiu's Sentence Changed to Death After Appeal

Wu Youshan, Zhang Desheng, Wang Asan, and Others' Appeals Rejected

Xu Leqing, a broker at the Gauze Exchange, was suddenly attacked by kidnappers near the Jing'an Temple bus stop last year. In an attempt to kidnap him, Cao was shot and killed due to Xu's resistance. Later, Chief Inspector Lu Liankui of the General Inspection Office and others arrested the kidnappers in this case: Wu Ziqiu, Wu Youshan, Zhang Desheng, Wang Asan, Wang Lao Jiu, Yao Zhifa, and more than ten others. They were sent to the First Special Court for questioning. Wang Lao Jiu and Yao Zhifa were sentenced to death and have already been executed by shooting. Wu Ziqiu was sentenced to 20 years in prison, and Wu Youshan, Zhang Desheng, and Wang Asan were each sentenced to 12 years in prison, as reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Wu Ziqiu and the other three were dissatisfied with the first instance verdict and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. The Court of Appeal held a hearing and questioned Wu and others about their reasons for appeal. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that the first instance verdict on the appellants had already been leniently reduced. Now they are still not satisfied and have appealed to your court. He requested that their sentences be increased. The debate was ordered to be closed. Yesterday morning, the date for the verdict arrived. Criminal Division Chief Yu Hua, along with Judges Zhao and Zhou, took the bench and announced the verdict: Wu Ziqiu's sentence was changed to death. The appeals of Wu Youshan, Zhang Desheng, Wang Asan, and others were rejected.

Daughter of Japanese Revolutionary Leader

Willing to Marry a Chinese Man

Indignant at the Evil Reputation of the "Traitor Ashikaga Takauji"'s Descendants

Willing to Abandon Her Noble Family and Come to Shanghai

Yesterday's Japanese-language Mainichi Shimbun reported that Ashikaga Tsune, the 26-year-old daughter of Baron Ashikaga at Sonokouchi, a Japanese revolutionary leader, married Zhu Lifu, the manager of the Dachang Refining and Dyeing Company at 566 Huade Road in the city. It is reported that Zhu graduated from the engineering department of Jinling University. Tsune was indignant at the evil reputation of "the descendants of the traitor Ashikaga Takauji" and was willing to abandon her noble family. During her school days, she changed her surname to Sugawara. After graduating, she became a Christian missionary. Later, her mood changed drastically, and she specialized in propagating communism among the Japanese aristocracy. At that time, she fell in love with party member Hisao Atsumi, but she felt quite restricted due to her noble family connections. In 1930, she came to Shanghai and attempted suicide at the Banzai Pavilion, but failed. She was introduced by Pastor Furuya to work as a nurse at the Fumin Hospital. However, because she believed in leftist ideologies, she used the hospital as a base to incite Chinese and Japanese nurses in the hospital and contacted Chinese and Japanese communists in Shanghai. She was later reported by the Consulate General and released shortly afterward. She then became a typist at the Shanghai branch of Mitsui & Co. and gradually became acquainted with Zhu Lifu. Now they have become a formal couple.

Major Fire on Zhongshan Road

—One Hundred Forty to Fifty Thatched Sheds Destroyed—

Around 1:30 AM yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the thatched shed inhabited by Tao Kun, a Jiangbei Yancheng native, next to the Toyota workshop on Zhongshan Road, north of the Fawangdu Ditch in western Shanghai. Thick smoke immediately filled the air and burst through the roof. The area was densely packed with thatched sheds, and with the strong winds, the fire quickly spread to the surrounding neighborhood. The fire was raging fiercely. When the Caojiadu and Zhabei fire brigades heard the alarm, they rushed to the scene with their fire engines. However, because the thatched sheds were easily flammable and the affected area was very wide, the fire was beyond control. After the firefighters fought hard to put out the fire for about an hour, it was finally extinguished. Yang Jinxiang, the police chief of the Zhongshan Bridge Police Station in the Sixth District, led the police to the scene to maintain order and immediately conducted an inspection. It was estimated that about 140 to 150 thatched sheds were destroyed, inhabited by over 100 households, half of whom were factory workers. They were all extremely poor. Old and young, men and women, were awakened from their dreams, their cries filled the air, and their condition was pitiable. Police Chief Yang immediately arrested Tao Kun, the person responsible for the fire, and witness Wang, and took them to the Sixth District for interrogation.

Hands Are Red

Is That a Communist Trait?

Fudan University Student Zhang Wenlie Arrested Because Of It

Anti-Fascist Leaflets Found in His Pocket

—Released on Bail Due to Lack of Other Evidence—

Zhang Wenlie, a student at Fudan University, was walking near the intersection of Avenue Annam and Jing'an Temple Road in western Shanghai the other day when he was suddenly identified by Kang Shounian, an informant of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, as a communist. He tried to arrest him. Zhang absolutely denied being a communist and refused to be captured. A struggle ensued. A patrolman saw the conflict and asked the reason. Each gave his own version. The patrolman took both parties to the Jing'an Temple Police Station. The police chief asked the informant how he knew Zhang was a communist. The informant said that Zhang's hands were red, which was a characteristic. He asked to search Zhang's person. The police chief searched Zhang and found two leaflets in his pocket with language opposing fascism. The pocket was torn. Zhang argued that the leaflets were not his and that the informant had put them in his pocket during the struggle to frame him. As for the redness of his hands, it was due to frostbite. The police chief sent detectives to Zhang's residence at No. 35, New Yuyuan Village, Yuyuan Road, to investigate, but found no evidence of reactionary activity. The next day, he was sent to the Second Branch of the High Court. The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent personnel to the court and requested a transfer, saying that Zhang's communist involvement was based on the confession of a captured communist. The court ordered Zhang to be detained for further investigation. Yesterday, Judge Yu of the Second Branch of the High Court and Judges Zhao and Zhou held a continued hearing. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin and defendant's defense lawyer Xue Dubi both appeared in court. The Municipal Public Security Bureau also brought a detained communist to testify in the case. Judge Yu questioned the defendant and witnesses one by one. Informant Kang Shounian then entered the witness stand and gave a long and impassioned statement. He even made remarks that infringed on the defense lawyer, saying that communists should not have lawyers to defend them. Now there is a lawyer who is a member of the Central Committee and was once the Minister of the Interior defending the communists, so he is no different from a communist. Lawyer Xue, hearing these words, believed that the informant deliberately insulted his personality in the solemn courtroom. He was furious and sternly questioned the informant, warning him not to make insinuations. The atmosphere in the court was tense. Judge Yu stopped it. The result of the investigation was that the court ruled that there was no need to transfer the case, and the defendant was released on bail.

Sudden Death of Young Woman

Determined to Be Due to Premortem Poisoning

Whether She Was Forced to Take Poison

Investigated by the Police Department

The late Zheng Yangchu from Chaoyang County, Guangdong, established two pawnshops, Wanfeng and Guanglifeng, at No. 69 Zhengjia Muqiao Street and No. 235 at the corner of Xizilaihuo Street, Caishi Street, in the French Concession. He accumulated assets of over 100,000 yuan. He died five years ago, leaving behind a wife and a concubine, both from the same hometown. The wife, Wu, is 40 years old this year, and the concubine, Huang, is 28 years old. Wu has a daughter, Xue'e, who is 20 years old this year, and adopted a son when her husband was alive, who is 18 years old this year. Huang did not have any children, and adopted a son, Jixian, who is 10 years old this year, after her husband's death. The wife and concubine live together in the new Guanglifeng store. Wu lives in the front building room, and Huang lives with her son and the eldest wife's daughter Xue'e in the three-story pavilion room. The wife and concubine live together, and they are usually harmonious. However, Huang, as a young widow, is often depressed and taciturn. After Zheng's death, the two pawnshops were entrusted to his eldest nephew Zheng Murong for management. In the summer of the year before last, Zheng Wu discovered that her nephew Zheng Murong had engaged in fraudulent activities in the two stores, amounting to over 10,000 yuan. She reported this to the police station and filed a public prosecution against Zheng Murong in the Second Special Court for embezzlement in his capacity. Murong also filed a civil suit, requesting a division of the property. Both cases have not yet been concluded. Members of the same clan have mediated, but the matter has not been resolved because Wu is unwilling to compromise. As a result, Wu has offended some people. Someone threw bombs and filth into the store to intimidate her. On the evening of the 13th, around 8 p.m., Zheng Huang accompanied her son to bed because he was ill. Unexpectedly, at 8:30 a.m. the next morning, Xue'e, the eldest wife Wu's daughter, got up and found Zheng Huang dead in bed. The news spread far and wide. Zheng Jinshun, Zheng Guoan, Zheng Jinzhi, and other nephews learned of the death and reported it to the French police station, saying that Zheng Huang's death was unclear. Because the eldest wife Zheng Wu was usually fierce and abusive, there was suspicion that she had been forced to take poison. They requested an investigation. The police station, after receiving the report, sent Detective Zhang Chunsheng to investigate. It was difficult to determine the truth. The body was taken to the autopsy room of the Tongren Fuyuan Branch. Yesterday, the police station reported to the Second Special District Court, which commissioned Prosecutor Wang Ren, along with forensic doctor Jiang Jun and clerk Peng Yu, to inspect the body at noon. An olive pit was dug out of the deceased's mouth, but the external shape could not reveal the truth of the death. The official took the bench and first heard the detective's report on the investigation of the case. He questioned Zheng Jinshun, who said that the deceased was his aunt and that he learned of her death from others. He did not know how she died. Zheng Wu, the eldest wife (whose testimony was translated by her daughter because she did not understand the Shanghai dialect), said that the deceased was her husband's concubine and that she did not know how she died. Zheng Xue'e (the eldest wife's daughter) said that the deceased was her stepmother. She took her son to sleep the night before. I slept in the same room, on the opposite bed. I went into the room at 11 o'clock and saw them sleeping soundly. I was doing needlework in the room for about an hour before going to sleep. At 5 o'clock yesterday morning, the younger brother (referring to the deceased's son) got up to urinate. I turned on the light for him. At 8:30, I got up to call her, but she did not respond. I pushed her, but she did not move. When I opened the quilt, I saw that her body was stiff. I was shocked and called my mother and the clerk to come and see, and then I knew she was dead. She liked to eat olives in the past. I don't know how she died, but there was no sound before she died. After verifying the testimony, Lord said that the cause of death could not be determined from the deceased's appearance and that an autopsy would be performed in the afternoon. Zheng Jinshun, Zheng Guoan, and Zheng Jinzhi, who reported the police station, submitted a statement to the court, requesting a detailed examination to respect human life. At 3:30 in the afternoon, Prosecutor Wang, Forensic Doctor Jiang, and Clerk Peng visited the room and performed an autopsy on the body. A small piece of opium dross, which had not yet dissolved, was found in the deceased's stomach. The liquid residue in the stomach was also poured out and smelled, and it had the smell of raw soil and alcohol. After the examination, the official took the bench again and questioned both parties of the deceased's family. It was determined that Zheng Huang died of opium poisoning before her death. The body was claimed by Zheng Wu, a member of the deceased's family. Whether Zheng Huang was forced to take poison will be investigated and handled by the Police Department.

National Products Industry

Today's Banquet for Needle Manufacturer Yin Zhizhong

Needle manufacturer Yin Zhizhong had an unusual talent in his youth and dedicated himself to industry. Soon after, he went to study abroad. Realizing that China's clothing needles had always been supplied by other countries, he felt ashamed. So, while studying, he studied needle manufacturing methods day and night. After eight years of hard work, he mastered all the techniques. After returning to China, he founded the Jilu Needle Factory in Qingdao and served as its manager. He carefully manufactured various sewing needles. The materials were excellent and comparable to imported products. They have been sold well in China and Southeast Asia and have established a good reputation. He also participated in various national products exhibitions. However, Yin is not satisfied with this. He often goes to various places to investigate the use of needles. He arrived in Shanghai last night and stayed at the New Asia Hotel. The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products and the Zhengyi Society, etc., specially held a banquet at the Zhengyi Society at No. 184 Nanjing Road today (16th) to welcome him, and invited celebrities from all walks of life to accompany him.
