*Shen Bao* Local Supplement

Commentary

The New Life Movement

— Shou Zi

Recently, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek launched the New Life Movement in Nanchang, the general idea of which is to take propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame as the center of life, and to be diligent, hard-working, honest, and disciplined, so that one can become a new citizen. This is a very meaningful thing.

At present, the lives of the Chinese people are indeed too "un-new." Greed, filth, shamelessness, and lowness, all the evils of mankind, have almost become the only popular atmosphere in our society now. If you don't eat, that's it, but if you want to eat, you must be greedy, filthy, shameless, and low. The more you eat, the more greedy, filthy, shameless, and low you become. This is truly a very heartbreaking phenomenon. Now that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is advocating the New Life Movement, with propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame as the center, it can be said to be prescribing the right medicine for the disease, which can somewhat reverse these trends.

However, I still have a point of view. The ancients said it well, "When clothing and food are sufficient, people know propriety and righteousness." It can be seen that if you want the people to "know propriety and righteousness," you must first make them able to have "sufficient clothing and food." "Sufficient clothing and food" is the only prerequisite for "knowing propriety and righteousness." It also says: "Teach after wealth." That is, to "teach" the people, you must first "enrich" the people. The meaning is the same as the previous sentence. Then, can most of our people now have "sufficient clothing and food"? Are they "rich"? Of course not. What we see is the bankruptcy of tens of millions of farmers, and the reduction of work or closure of batches of factories. What the people need most now seems to be only the two words "clothing and food." Under these circumstances, whether it is possible to promote propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame seems to be somewhat problematic. I am not saying that it is impossible to promote propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame under the current circumstances, but rather that before promoting propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, one should pay a little attention to the people's livelihood problems. Because this is an important prerequisite for promoting propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. Therefore, I hope that after launching the meaningful New Life Movement, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will come up with an even more meaningful policy that will enable the general public to have "sufficient clothing and food" and to be "rich." If this is the case, then Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's contributions to the people will be unattainable. This is one.

Secondly, in addition to the fact that the lives of the general public are too "un-new," the general social phenomena in our country are also too un-new. Red pills, white flour, opium, extortionate taxes, miscellaneous taxes, corrupt officials, dirty officials, local tyrants, evil gentry, floods, droughts, wars, and the infighting of military personnel in various places (such as the Guizhou War, the conflict between Sun and Ma, and the Sichuan War that just stopped not long ago), have made the people no longer have new hope, and society no longer has a bright place. These are the reasons that make our society uniquely "un-new." If we really want to make our people new and live a new life, I think the above-mentioned sources of poison must be completely removed first. If these sources of poison are not removed, I am afraid that the people will not be able to become new. Society is a mass of darkness, and the people are living in abject poverty. Where can new light arise from? Therefore, I hope that after advocating the New Life Movement, the wise Chairman Chiang Kai-shek will come up with an even more meaningful task of how to thoroughly realize the New Life. I think Chairman Chiang Kai-shek has probably already taken this into account. This is two.

The above is my opinion. Finally, I hope that all Chinese people will support this New Life Movement. And even more support Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in how to further make this New Life thoroughly realized, that is, how to make the people have "sufficient clothing and food," how to make the people "rich," and how to thoroughly eliminate the unique sources of poison that prevent this society from becoming "new." This is an important task. And only in this way can the New Life Movement become more meaningful.

Little Life

— Shu Xian

Only a week after giving birth, she bravely struggled to go back to work in the factory. On the one hand, the factory had already used up her limited leave. On the other hand, she was willing to earn a little more wage herself, so she could do something more for her only little life.

Before dawn, without waiting for the factory's sharp whistle to urge her, she automatically got out of bed, hastily ate two bowls of cold rice, and hurriedly picked up the sleeping infant from the warm quilt. She lovingly and sweetly kissed his round little face, tightly wrapped him with a dozen pieces of rags, and carried him out of the door, bathing in the faint light of the sparse morning stars, walking towards the factory on the quiet, long road.

She is now a mother with a son! Her infinite happiness and hope for the future are all on this son. She must work harder to raise him well, cherish him, and for him, she would rather endure all the suffering that others cannot endure! She thought this way as she walked.

In the dim light of dawn, one can vaguely see the towering factory chimney and the terrifying black smoke that pours from the window and streams diagonally across the sky. Before she was swallowed by the factory's iron gate, which looked like a gaping blood mouth, she tightly covered the infant's head with two pieces of rags, then pretended to be calm and walked slowly past the gatekeeper with shining eyes, indicating that the package did not contain a secretly smuggled infant, but some other object.

Having sneaked through the factory gate, she breathed a sigh of relief and walked straight into the workshop. Many sisters curiously gathered around, all vying to take a look. Praises, congratulations, and envious sighs

Page 22

, a cacophony of voices.

It was time for the shift change! The sisters gradually dispersed to busy themselves with their own work. She opened a cover plate under the machine and stuffed the little life into the gap in the machine's belly.

This is the most proper method for female workers in the factory to secretly feed their children. The machine's belly is also the only secret cradle for those female workers' children. The machine's wheels quickly rotate next to the child's body, and dark purple machine oil drips onto the child's body and head, but this will not cause any unexpected danger, as long as the mother's binding skills are skillful, the child will lie inside motionless as if listening. In the noisy machine shop, the child's crying cannot be heard at all, and the tender child will naturally fall asleep from the strong vibration of the machine. Therefore, as long as the breastfeeding is done discreetly, it is very difficult for factory staff to detect it.

Nine o'clock arrived! It was the time for the staff to change shifts and rest. So she first asked many sisters to serve as sentries in all directions, then gathered many sisters to tightly surround her, quickly opened the machine cover plate, and carefully took the little treasure out of the machine's belly to breastfeed. As soon as the nipple was put into the infant's small mouth, she suddenly heard an emergency signal from the sentry. Everyone knew that the staff was coming, and hurriedly hid the infant again, and everyone dispersed.

After work, when she dragged the infant out of the machine's belly, she found that the infant had a strange abnormality. The eyes were so dull, the small breaths were so rapid that she was afraid, and the rosy little face had also turned ashen pale. Only then did she remember that someone had warned her when she entered the factory that a seven-day-old infant should not be brought into the factory. So she trembled! She saw boundless darkness coming upon her.

When she passed through the first card door, she stuffed a silver dollar into the hand of the woman who searched her. The woman smiled cunningly and nodded slightly to her. She was then let go.

After leaving the factory gate, she ran home in one breath. When she looked at the infant more carefully, the infant's breathing had already stopped! But she did not cry, she only shouted "Heaven", and her body collapsed onto the little corpse.

The Story of a Street Urchin (9)

— Produced by Chen Jingsheng

Good fellow, such powerful little tricks

The Metaphor of Life

— Jianshe

Watching those countrymen who, once holding a policeman's baton, spare no effort in beating the Jiangbei elders, astonishment is always unavoidable. Originally, one would think that the countryman is also Chinese, and the Jiangbei elder is also Chinese. With only a slight difference in region, there is such a bad feeling, which is indeed worthy of astonishment. Because the general countrymen's notion is that countrymen are like-minded.

However, I still want to say that those who hold this view do not understand the philosophy of maggots at all.

If we pass through the countryside and pay attention to the rural manure tanks, we can definitely find small white worms that are twice as long as rice on the edge of the tank, and these are maggots. If we pay even more attention, we can definitely discover that these small white maggots are not stationary on the edge of the tank, but are constantly, tirelessly, vigorously climbing towards the very top of the tank edge.

There is no need to doubt that their upward climbing has a pure and profound meaning. Because once they climb out of the tank edge, they can undergo a metamorphosis, that is, live in the black pupal shell for a few days, and then transform into a buzzing fly that can fly. And there is no need to doubt that this is social advancement!

Originally, being a maggot is not very remarkable; and there are so many maggots. And all they eat is the manure pile, manure. To be able to step over the heads of other maggots, treat other fellow creatures as stepping stones for their own upward climb, and climb all the way to the edge of the tank, undergoing metamorphosis, so that the body is fat, and they can fly, and they can approach the most lovable and sweetest things in the world as they please, which maggot wouldn't want that?

From our point of view, a fly is not necessarily more remarkable than a maggot. However, some maggots clearly do not think this way. And this is the difference between maggots and us, and it is also what is called the philosophy of maggots.

To understand the philosophy of maggots is of course to understand the meaning of maggots wanting to climb onto the edge of the tank, but thinking that a maggot is so rare to climb onto the manure tank, they may also feel the blandness of this life!

Also Discussing the Rent Reduction Movement

— Wu

Recently, white banners with blue characters have often been found on the streets, written in a very neat official script, and the wording is also very fresh, the most prominent being "To prosper Shanghai, you must first reduce rents." This slogan is naturally very legal, otherwise it would inevitably be like the black characters on the utility poles, covered with a layer of lime. Vaguely, like an eighteen-year-old young lady wearing a pink silk gauze dress. But the former does not enchant people, but instead arouses a sense of righteous indignation. Because of this righteous banner, people cannot help but think of the "January 28th" incident, when stores posted "Brutal troops invade, strike to resist insults" at their doors, and later, the "long-term resistance, open for business with pain." Although the antithetical couplets are not as well-balanced as similar spring couplets such as "Favorable weather for crops, the nation is prosperous and the people are at peace," their style is quite similar to spring couplets, assuming that the sound of the cannons is the sound of firecrackers.

Let's get back to the topic, then, the rent reduction slogan is not just a perfunctory official document. And it also gives people a sense of justice. However, soon after, I read a great article from a group of heroes and good men, saying that to prosper Shanghai, you must first "pacify the interior." There is probably an unparalleled reason, but unfortunately, I cannot understand it and do not remember it. However! In this way, the so-called prosperity becomes quite problematic. So I also thought about this issue.

From the perspective of general patriots, perhaps they think very thoroughly. For example, the current market is depressed, and "massive discounts" and "15% off" banners adorn the New Year of singing and dancing; if rents are reduced by two yuan, it will increase purchasing power by two yuan, so domestic goods can be revitalized, and the market will become more prosperous day by day, and store owners will smile happily; isn't it like giving a dying patient a shot of morphine? But attempting to prosper Shanghai with the blood of "bandits" ultimately feels like the bloody smell is too strong, only cannibals would be so ferocious. It's really scary to talk about.

People who live in Shanghai probably know very well that Shanghai's rents are indeed shockingly expensive. It goes without saying that a three-story building costs eighty-five taels a month or a large厢房 costs fifty yuan, but a small pavilion room that can only fit an iron bed and a typewriter in the Beijing Road area costs ten yuan, in Caojiadu it also costs seven yuan, and one with pasted floral paper costs fourteen yuan or more.

I once had a friend who was learning to paint, and he rented a small pavilion room for ten yuan a month. Because he was learning to paint, he used charcoal to draw nude women on the white wall. I asked him, "Why are you doing this?" He replied angrily, "I have lived here for one year, a total of one hundred and twenty yuan, which is enough to build this small house, which means I bought it, why can't I paint?" This statement is very reasonable, and the extent of his anger can be imagined.

Furthermore, if a husband and wife both work, they can earn fifteen yuan a month in total, averaging five 角大洋 per day, and the rent takes away two 角三分强, what is enough for the remaining two 角六分? Each person eating two bowls of Yangchun noodles a day also costs 大洋 two 角, plus three seven two hundred and ten 文, even including drinking ball brand water... Calculated in this way, the rent takes away half of the income. Spending twelve hours a day in the factory inhaling cotton dust is equivalent to working six hours for the landlord. This is of course happy for the bloated vampires, and half of the workers' flesh and blood fly out of the chimney for the real estate developers. If the industry is already like this, then the unemployed are crying even more bitterly. No work, no food, but the rent must always be paid, otherwise they will be locked up in the Public Security Bureau to uphold the national law.

Therefore, the rent reduction movement is more of a rescue for the workers than a prosperity for Shanghai!

The Humor of the National Socialist Party

— Zhong

The task of the National Socialist Party, as explained by Rosenberg, the director of foreign affairs of the National Socialist Party, is stated precisely as follows -

"What the National Socialist Party proclaims to the people, and what it requires of the people, does not require that 60 million German people all agree with it; the main point is that the German people must all take the same attitude! Approximately, one of the ideas that General Hitler has believed in for the longest time will surely be realized one day - what is the idea? That is, the movement of the National Socialist Party will one day become crystallized, and can be represented by an order - this order represents absolute authority, and the party's command is executed by this order!"

Berlin, 3rd, Havas telegram.

This speech is truly the pinnacle of euphemism and circumlocution. Before the next sentence is spoken, the explanation of the next sentence is spoken first. It can be said that the party is extremely careful and capable!

In a word!! "Hitler's orders must be uniformly obeyed and followed by all German people."!! So what is the task of the National Socialist Party? Hitler issues orders for the benefit of a minority! This is the task of all tasks.

We cannot believe in Hitler-style orders.

We can find a political formula for the National Socialist Party here!!

"The party's command" is "absolute authority". "Absolute authority" is "order". "Order" is "the idea that Hitler has believed in for the longest time"!! That is, the idea of ​​the steel magnate behind the scenes.

The above is an abstract formula, let us establish a concrete formula!!

This is the most central political policy of the National Socialist Party.

It's Hard to Be an Official

— Guang Nan

After thinking it over, it's still more advantageous for a person to be an official. Promotion and wealth have always been the two major goals of Chinese people, but in fact, these two are related. With promotion, one can naturally become wealthy, and with wealth, there will definitely be official promotion, which is precisely two in one. Therefore, I only choose one. However, being an official is sometimes not easy. For example, recently Chairman Chiang Kai-shek issued an order to strictly prohibit banquets, smoking, and gambling, and the two chairmen of Henan and Shandong are also promoting vigor, which is truly a great misfortune for the officialdom. Just imagine, being an official but not being able to indulge in wine and food, and having to get up at dawn, what kind of official is that? Is this kind of official good to be?

When a person becomes an official, 洋房, cars, and women should all be available. It is unreasonable not to think about enjoyment. Moreover, when a person becomes an official, relatives and friends will naturally increase, so socializing and entertaining is inevitable, how can one avoid banquets, smoking, and gambling? But Chairman Chiang Kai-shek does not think so, saying something like "Worry can lead to survival, while joy invites calamity," encouraging people to "be vigilant and diligent, and to reflect on themselves," not allowing "indulging in wine and food, nor considering laziness as a good plan," even smoking and gambling are strictly prohibited, believing that these two "consume ambition and waste time, truly great misfortunes that ruin the country and the family," doesn't this disappoint people greatly?

Now that the ways for officials to enjoy themselves have been banned, then every official sits in the office from morning till night, busy all day (?), sleeping in a few hours in the morning is not considered laziness, or even being able to rush to the office during the prescribed office hours can be said to be fulfilling one's duty. How could they know that the two chairmen of Henan and Shandong even want to deprive them of this little bit of leisure, calling on people to "rise at the sound of the rooster," saying that this is to "promote vigor and strengthen the body," isn't it extremely unlucky?

In recent China, everything has really changed, even being an official is a bit difficult!

To My Friend

— Zhi

Received your letter from the edge of West Lake, so passionate, so indignant, so sad, and so gently expressing a cry of sorrow for life!

Since things are difficult to your liking, it is good to go back for a while, but going back will make you even sadder. My meaning is that you should endure the current pain, do not be too emotional, this era will never give us a day of comfort, as long as there is a central point to support life, you can hold on to it and not let go. For the regret that your past efforts have not yielded results, although it is human nature, it is also unnecessary. Friend, I want to warn you: if the heart of regret is too strong, the feeling of disappointment will be deep, and if the fire of being a person is completely extinguished, then the ending will naturally only be a path of suicide and self-abandonment.

Your and Shushan's life experiences are quite similar, and your personalities are somewhat alike in many ways. Shushan committed suicide, and to this day we still deeply hide an irreparable wound. When a group of us gather together to remember Shushan's death, we still can't hold back the tears of crying together at home! You should think deeply about this sad scene, and the thought of suicide and self-abandonment may re-stir up waves in your brain.

I often say: a pessimistic person has strength, a courageous, thorough, and positive attitude towards life. People who give up on themselves, or even commit suicide, are too optimistic about the world. Optimism easily leads to disappointment, easily leads to negativity, easily leads people to fall into a circle of sadness, unable to extricate themselves.

We should be people of society, people of the nation, people of the world. Many things are crippled in the personal aspect, but looking at the whole, they emit brilliance. People with rich emotions cannot but treat this kind of empty talk as their own ideal and live by it. Do you have such an ideal? You are now in a real life, you must not question the foundation of life because of current disappointments!

Amateur Mailbox

Face Turns Green

Editor Sir:

In the amateur mailbox column of the supplement of this newspaper, I often see many difficult questions, all of which are answered in detail by you. This really makes me admire and respect you. Now I have a difficult matter, please do not abandon me and give me a concrete answer!

The matter is as follows:

My father is a clerk in a factory in his sixties. In the past (three years ago), he opened a small company. This was jointly established with the capital of nine shareholders. My father had the most shares, so he was appointed manager by the shareholders. Unfortunately, after doing it for two or three years, due to poor sales and low prices, it was closed down at a loss. In addition to losing all of his own shares, my father was also responsible for repaying the shareholders' shares at that time.

After a year, my father, due to the heavy pressure of share debts and the compulsion of life, entrusted a relative to introduce him, and dragged his aging body into the factory to work. In less than a year, I was also introduced by a relative to work in the same factory as my father, as a trainee. At that time, I was exactly seventeen years old.

Because the salary is too small to pay for the expenses at home, it is even impossible to repay the shareholders' debts. We can often receive letters from shareholders urging us to pay.

Recently, I received a letter containing... "I hope to pay off the debts within these few days, otherwise, I will come to your house to sit, eat, and live, and report to the officialdom for investigation," and so on. My father was stunned and his face turned green after reading it at that time. Therefore, as his son, seeing my father so anxious, I had to ask for your advice.

Sir: Is there any legal basis for this? I am waiting for your reply. Respectfully wish

Zhuo An Hua Yafu respectfully

Editor's note: When the partnership property is insufficient to pay off debts, each partner should bear joint and several liability in accordance with Article 681 of the Civil Code. If Mr. Hua's father can provide evidence of the partnership, and that the store's loss was not caused by his deliberate or negligent acts, then he is not liable for compensation for the shares, and the partners cannot "come to your house to sit, eat, and live."

By mail: To Ms. Lan Fen: The purpose of the job introduction in this publication is to facilitate the general unemployed. If you want to publish it, please send a letter to the amateur weekly of this newspaper.

Novel

Lulu's Victory (10) (2)

— Translated by Jingxin, written by Italian M. Saice Ao

One evening Lulu walked into her room. "Would you help me with something?" she asked.

"What is it?"

"I have some notes to take," Lulu said. "Robert is alone on the balcony outside. Would you be willing to keep him company?"

"But I!!"

"Would you rather be locked up in here alone? Is it so difficult to do something for me?"

"Will you be here soon?"

"I just need to write four lines."

Sophia turned to the balcony, mustering her courage for this punishment. She stopped at the door. Robert was walking back and forth; she walked towards him.

"Lulu told me to come," she said in a low voice.

"You came reluctantly, didn't you?"

"Reluctantly!!"

Every fiber of her body was trembling; Robert was approaching her, his face deformed by desire.

"What have I done to make you dislike me, Sophia?"

"Nothing at all. Please don't look at me like that," she pleaded, frightened.

"Then, Sophia, you know that I love you very much."

"Ah! Don't say that, Robert, for God's sake, don't say that! What if Lulu hears!"

"I don't love Lulu. I love you, Sophia."

"You are deceiving."

"I know, but I love you. I want to leave!!"

"Oh! Lulu cried out in the distance, appearing at another door. "Oh, are you two quiet?"

But no one answered. Sophia fled, her face hidden in her hands; Robert stood there motionless, silent, as if he had fainted.

"Robert!" Lulu called out.

"Lulu."

"What's wrong with you?"

"Nothing; I want to go."

Without even saying goodbye to her, he thought about the appearance of despair, Lulu's eyes followed him.

Standing there, lost in thought.
